 vikaas ke paas saare dukhon kaa jawaab he or bharti apane bhai kii naukari jane se dukhi he
 Vikas explains that it will be found, but think, millions of people do not get work in villages, so the government has made MNREGA with a 2005 law
 manaregaa kaarykram nahin, ek kanoon he
 Under this law, anyone can ask for work from his sarpanch and if he does not get work in 15 days, he will also get unemployment allowance
 vikaas ke jariye yah kaarykram manaregaa ke makasad ko bataane lagata he
 Bharti is surprised by these things of development that work will get in MNREGA only when someone asks for work
 naseeb ke bharose kaam nahin miltaa he
 After this Vikas tells Bharati the story of Sumer and Sumati
 satyanarayan puja kii tarj par katha shuru hoti he ki kaam na milane ke kaaran sumer or sumati pareshaan the
 They feel that only the people of Sarmpach get work in MNREGA, so instead of going to Sarpanch, Sumer will work in the city
 un donon ko baahar jate sarpanch sahab dekh lete hai or kehete hai ki jab tum kaam maang sakate ho to baahar kyon ja rahe ho
 Come to the Gram Sabha and fill a form, you will get some work or the other, but you will get the work only when you ask
 dilli kii sadak par car chalaate-chalaate manaregaa kaa yah kaarykram thodi der ke liye isse jude raajnneetik vivaadon main bhi le gaya
 After coming home, i started to google
 jis manaregaa ko pradhanmantri ne gadde khudwane kaa kaarykram kahkar mazaaq udaaya tha, unheen kii sarkaar ke is kaarykram main manaregaa ko lekar gaanaa he ki ab chalaa vikaas gaanv kii raah
 Vikas tells Bharti that if someone's house is being built under Indira Awaas Yojana, then wages can also be got due to MNREGA
 raajnneeti jo bhi ho, manaregaa kaa bachaa rahanaa zyaada zaruri he
 i liked this program
 bas, iske jariye yah bhi bataaya jaataa ki kitni mazaduri milegi, berojgaare bhatta kahaan se milegaa, kitne din main milegaa, mazaduron ke adhikaar kya hai
 There are reports that MNREGA does not even get full wages
 copiriter ne manaregaa kii mazaduri ko aise pesh kiya he, jaise yah nunatam mazaduri na hokar kisi siio kii tankhwaah ho
 MNREGA wages are being linked to better lives, such as Sumer and Sumati will book flats in Noida Extension
 copiraiteron ko samajhnaa chahie ki manaregaa sirf buniyadi zarurat kaa kaarykram he
 a hundred days a year does not improve one's life, his work is definitely done
 sarkaar ko bataanaa chahie ki manaregaa kii puri mazaduri na milane par mazdoor kya kar saktaa he
 The Modi government has given 12 percent more money - 34,669 crore in the MNREGA compared to the previous financial year
 google kiya to ek or khabar nikal ai
 On May 7, 15 opposition mps in the Lok Sabha asked the government to send the money of MNREGA to the states soon
 gramin vikaas mantri virendra singh ne jawaab diya ki 12,000 karod rupee bheje ja chuke hai, lekin kaam na milane par berojgaare bhatta dene kii baat he, vah rajya sarkaar kii zimmedaari he
 Mallikarjun Kharge of Congress in Lok Sabha said that Rajasthan and Madhya Pradesh have also complained that money is not being received from the Center
 hamen nahin pataa chal rahaa he ki sach koun bol rahaa he
 The agency reported on 23 April this year that under MGNREGA, workdays in 2014-15 have been reduced from 46 to 40 as compared to the previous year, whereas 100 days should be done
 kendriya gramin vikaas rajyamantri ne loksabhaa main kaha ki aisa isliye hua he ki manaregaa maang par aadhaarit kaarykram he
 Demand has declined for several reasons
 yah sab isliye bataaya ki manaregaa ko lekar ati ashavad se bachanaa chahie
 Government programs should also be built on practical ground
 aalochak is baat se khush ho sakate hai ki sarkaar manaregaa ko apnaane lagi he
 Now she does not see MNREGA as associated with UPA, so Vividh Bharati sponsored program is already said that this is the 2005 law
 itani eemaandaaree bhi kam nahin hoti
 The Prime Minister has launched Kisan TV for the farmers of the country
 yah ek acha kadam he, meri dua he ki yah channel safal ho
 i also spoke to Prasar Bharati chairman a Suryaprakash
 unhone bataaya ki kisaan channel par desh ke ek hazaar mandiyon ke bhav bijness channel kii tarj par neeche kii pattiyon par chalaa karenge
 The farmers of the country will come to know together and at the same time
 iske alaava mausam vibhaag ke sahyog se mausam kii jaankaree di jaaegi
 There will also be a half-hour program daily on the weather
 kisaan ko yahaan tak bataaya jayega ki bulandshahr yaa panipat main mausam thik he or ve agle hafte se buvaai kar sakate hai
 The Meteorological Department has an estimate of five days in every district of the country
 suryaprakash ne kaha ki hamane iske liye nai team banaai he or puraa focus is baat par hoga ki kisaan ke chashme se kheti ko dekha jaae
 The success of this channel will depend a lot on how the government encourages farmers for alternative farming through this
 modi sarkaar kaa argenic kheti kaa vaada bhi he, jisaki charchaa bhi sunai nahin detii he
 There is only apprehension that this channel may not fall prey to the seeds and technology tactics of multinational companies, as it is the first channel in the country that will talk directly to the farmers
 is gambhir ashanka se alaava kisaan channel se ummid hi zyaada he
 It is to be hoped that this will be openly debated on agricultural policies
 isse pehle bhi kai logon ne kheti se judaa akhbaar nikaalane kaa prayaas kiya he
 In Maharashtra, the 'sakal Group' has an agricultural newspaper 'agro One', which the farmers keep
 isamen kaam karne vaale kai samvaadadaata krishi-snaatak hote hai
 Similarly, a newspaper named 'krishkonnati' is coming out of Akola
 geetkaar neelesh misra bhi 'gaanv conection' (disclemur - isamen meraa bhi kollam aata he) ke naam se akhbaar nikaalte hai
 There is a need to emphasize farming, farming and village
 tippaniyan i do not want to disturb the color, but seeing the picture of the plow in the hands of the Prime Minister, it seemed that it was not the same solution which was given to Rahul Gandhi at Ramlila Maidan
 raajnneetik manchon par hal kii maujuudagi kii nirantarata kaa zikr itnaa bataane ke liye kiya ki hal ab kisaan kii pahchaan nahin he
 In many villages, the solution will not be seen
 chandrabhan prasad apane shodh se dikhaa chuke hai ki uttar pradesh ke purvi ilaake main hal samaapt ho chukaa he
 It has a significance
 raajnneetik or aarthik donon
 Along with the plow, the harava has also disappeared
 ham hal ke naam par kitna hi kisaan-kisaan kar len, lekin sachai yah he ki hal uthaane vaale kisaan dalit hote the or unke saath barabari kaa vyavhaar nahin hota tha
 Therefore, the next time both Prime Minister Narendra Modi and Rahul Gandhi do a program of farming, do not hold a solution
 hal ab samaadhaan nahin he
 In the film 'upkar', Manoj Kumar took the plow and converted it into a nationalist symbol and in the era of Lal Bahadur Shastri's 'jai Jawan Jai Kisan', the plow also became the symbol of some parties, but the plow and plow parties Both have disappeared
 hal or harvaahee hamaare samaaj ke shoshan kii tasviir he, na ki mahanata kii

 This program of MNREGA while driving a car on Delhi's road also took some time for political controversies related to it
 ghar aakar main google karne laga
 The MGNREGA, which the Prime Minister had mocked as a program of digging the pit, in this program of his government, there is a song about MNREGA that now the path of development village
 vikaas bharti ko kahata he ki agar indira awaas yojana ke tahat kisi kaa ghar ban rahaa ho to usamen bhi manaregaa ke chalate mazaduri mil sakati he
 Whatever may be the politics, survival of the MNREGA is more important
 mujhe to yah kaarykram acha laga
 Just through this, it is also told that from how much wages will be received, where will we get unemployment allowance, in how many days, what are the rights of the workers
 khabaren aati rahati hai ki manaregaa kii puri mazaduri bhi nahin milti he
 The copywriter has presented MGNREGA wages as if it were the salary of a CEO rather than the minimum wage
 manaregaa kii mazaduri ko behatar zindagi se aise joda ja rahaa he, jaise sumer or sumati noida ekstansion main flats book kara lenge
 Copywriters should understand that MNREGA is just a program of basic need
 saal main sau din ke rojgaar se kisi kii zindagi behatar nahin hoti, uskaa kaam zarur chal jaataa he
 The government should tell what the laborers can do if they do not get the full wages of MNREGA
 modi sarkaar ne manaregaa main pichley vitt varsh kii tulana main 12 pratishat zyaada paisa diya he - 34,669 karod
 When Google did, another news came out
 7 may ko loksabhaa main 15 vipakshi saansadon ne sarkaar se kaha ki manaregaa kaa paisa rajyon ko jaldi bheja jaae
 Rural Development Minister Virendra Singh replied that Rs 12,000 crore had been sent, but the matter of giving unemployment allowance if work is not available is the responsibility of the state government
 loksabhaa main congress ke mallikarjun khadge ne kaha ki rajasthan or madhya pradesh ne bhi shikaayat kii he ki centre se paisa nahin mil rahaa he
 We do not know who is telling the truth
 isi saal 23 april kii agency kii khabar he ki manaregaa ke tahat 2014-15 main kaarydiwas pichley saal kii tulana main 46 se kam hokar 40 ho gaye hai, jabaki hone chahie 100 din
 The Union Minister of State for Rural Development said in the Lok Sabha that this has happened because MNREGA is a demand-driven program
 kai kaarnon se maang main kami ai he
 All this was told that extreme optimism about MNREGA should be avoided
 sarkari kaaryakramon ko bhi vyaavhaarik dharaatal par banaaya janaa chahie
 Critics may be happy that the government is adopting the MNREGA
 ab vah manaregaa ko upie se jodakar nahin dekhati he, isliye vividh bharti ke pryojit kaarykram main pehle hi kaha jaataa he ki yah varsh 2005 kaa kanoon he
 Even this honesty does not diminish
 pradhanmantri ne desh ke kisaanon ke liye kisaan tivi launch kiya he
 This is a good step, i wish this channel is successful
 maine prasar bharti ke chairman e suryaprakash se baat bhi kii
 He informed that the prices of one thousand mandis of the country on the farmers channel will run on the bottom lines along the lines of the business channel
 desh ke kisaanon ko ek saath or ek hi samay main pataa chal jayega
 Apart from this, weather information will be given in collaboration with Meteorological Department
 mausam par rose aadhe ghante kaa kaarykram bhi hoga
 The farmer will even be told that the weather in Bulandshahr or Panipat is fine and they can sow from next week
 mausam vibhaag ke paas desh ke har zile ke paanch dinon kaa anumaan hota he
 Suryaprakash said that we have formed a new team for this and the entire focus will be on seeing agriculture through the glasses of the farmer
 is channel kii kamyaabi bahut kuch is baat par nirbhar karegi ki sarkaar iske jariye kisaanon ko vaikalpik kheti ke liye kaise protsaahit karti he
 There is also the promise of organic farming by the Modi government, which is not even heard of
 ek hi ashanka he ki kahin yah channel bahurashtriya companiyon ke beej or takanic ke hatkande kaa shikaar na ho jaae, kyonki yah desh kaa pehla channel he, jo sidhe kisaanon se baat karegaa
 Apart from this serious apprehension, there is more hope from the farmers channel
 ummid kii jaani chahie ki is par krishi nitiyon par khulkar bahes hogi
 Even before this, many people have tried to get a newspaper related to farming
 maharashtra main 'sakaal group' kaa ek krishi akhbaar he 'agro van', jise kisaan sahejkar rakhte hai
 Many correspondents working in it are agricultural graduates
 isi tarah akola se 'krishakonnati' naam se ek akhbaar nikal rahaa he
 Lyricist Nilesh Misra also publishes newspapers in the name of 'village Connection' (disclaimer - i also have a column in it)
 kheti, kisaani or gaanv par jor dene kii zarurat he
 The comments main rang main bhang nahin daalana chahta, lekin pradhanmantri ke haath main hal kii tasviir dekhakar laga ki yah vahi hal to nahin, jo ramlila maidan main rahul gandhi ko diya gaya tha
 The mention of the continuity of the plow's presence on political platforms was so much to show that the plow is no longer the identity of the farmer
 kai gaanvon main to hal dikhegaa bhi nahin
 Chandrabhan Prasad has shown through his research that the plow is over in the eastern part of Uttar Pradesh
 iskaa ek mahatv he
 Both political and economic
 hal ke saath-saath harvaahee bhi mit gai he
 No matter how many farmers and farmers we do in the name of plow, the truth is that the plow farmers used to be Dalits and they were not treated equally
 isliye pradhanmantri narendra modi or rahul gandhi donon agali baar jab kheti kaa koi kaarykram karen to hal na thaamen
 The solution is no longer the solution
